i would argue , again , opensource security is about connecting the international , the interagency , the privatepublic , and lashing it together with strategic communication , largely in social networks .	我想再次強調 , 開放式安全是關乎國際的 , 國際的 , 跨部門的 , 私人的和公共的 , 並和策略性的溝通 , 交流多半在社交網路上 。
so let me talk a little bit about why we need to do that , because our global commons is under attack in a variety of ways , and none of the sources of threat to the global commons will be solved by building walls .	所以 , 讓我來談談為什麼我們需要這麼做 , 因為我們的全球公有物正受到各種方式的攻擊 , 沒有威脅到全球公有物的來源 , 都會透過築牆來解決 。
now , i'm a sailor , obviously .	現在 , 我是一個水手 , 顯然
this is a ship , a liner , clipping through the indian ocean .	這是一艘船 , 一艘拖船 , 在印度洋上航行 。
what's wrong with this picture ?	這張圖有什麼問題 ?
it's got concertina wire along the sides of it .	沿著它的邊緣有鋼索 ,
that's to prevent pirates from attacking it .	也就是防止海盜來襲擊
piracy is a very active threat today around the world . this is in the indian ocean .	海盜是當今世界各地極為活躍的威脅 。 這是在印度洋 。
piracy is also very active in the strait of malacca .	海盜在馬拉卡的海峽也很活躍
it's active in the gulf of guinea .	活躍在幾內亞灣 ,
we see it in the caribbean .	我們看到在加勒比海
it's a $10billionayear discontinuity in the global transport system .	在全球運輸系統中 , 每一百億美金的不連續性會造成影響 。
last year , at this time , there were 20 vessels , 500 mariners held hostage .	去年 , 在這個時期 , 有20艘船 , 500名船員被挾持人質 。
this is an attack on the global commons .	這是對全球公有物的攻擊 。
we need to think about how to address it .	我們需要考慮如何解決
let's shift to a different kind of sea , the cyber sea .	讓我們轉到另一種海洋 , 網路的海洋 。
here are photographs of two young men .	這裡有兩個年輕人的照片 。
at the moment , they're incarcerated .	在當下 , 他們被監禁在
they conducted a credit card fraud that netted them over 10 billion dollars .	他們做了一個信用卡詐騙案 , 讓他們淨賺了超過一百億美元 。
this is part of cybercrime which is a $2trillionayear discontinuity in the global economy .	這是網路犯罪的一部分 , 是全球經濟兩萬億美元的不連續性 。
two trillion a year .	每年兩兆 。
that's just under the gdp of great britain .	那只是在英國的gdp之下 。
so this cyber sea , which we know endlessly is the fundamental piece of radical openness , is very much under threat as well .	所以 , 我們所知的網路海 , 無止境地是激進開放的基本元素 , 也受到很大的威脅 。
another thing i worry about in the global commons is the threat posed by trafficking , by the movement of narcotics , opium , here coming out of afghanistan through europe over to the united states .	我擔心的另一件事是全球公有物的威脅 , 由販賣 , 麻醉劑 , 鴉片的移動 , 從阿富汗穿過歐洲到美國 。
we worry about cocaine coming from the andean ridge north .	我們擔心從andeanridge北部運過來的可卡因 。
we worry about the movement of illegal weapons and trafficking . above all , perhaps , we worry about human trafficking , and the awful cost of it .	我們擔心非法武器的運輸 。 最重要的是 , 我們擔心人口販賣 , 以及它的可怕成本 。
trafficking moves largely at sea but in other parts of the global commons .	販賣行為的主要是在海上 , 但在全球公有物的其他部分 。
this is a photograph , and i wish i could tell you that this is a very hightech piece of us navy gear that we're using to stop the trafficking .	這是一張照片 , 我希望能告訴你們 , 這是非常高科技的美國海軍設備 , 我們用它來阻止人口販賣 。
the bad news is , this is a semisubmersible run by drug cartels .	壞消息是 , 這是一個販毒集團的半潛水器 。
it was built in the jungles of south america .	建在南美洲叢林中的
we caught it with that lowtech raft — — and it was carrying six tons of cocaine .	我們用低科技的木筏捕捉牠 , 牠帶著六噸的可卡因 。
crew of four . sophisticated communications sweep .	四個隊員 , 精良的溝通都掃了起來
this kind of trafficking , in narcotics , in humans , in weapons , god forbid , in weapons of mass destruction , is part of the threat to the global commons .	這種販賣 , 在毒品領域 , 在人、武器、被禁止 , 在大規模殺傷性武器中 , 都是造成全球公有物的威脅的一部分 。
and let's pull it together in afghanistan today .	並且讓我們今天在阿富汗一起拉吧 。
this is a field of poppies in afghanistan .	這是在阿富汗的一個熱鬧區 。
eighty to 90 percent of the world's poppy , opium and heroin , comes out of afghanistan .	世界上80%到90%的盆栽 , 鴉片和海洛因來自阿富汗 。
we also see there , of course , terrorism .	當然 , 我們也看到恐怖主義 。
this is where al qaeda is staged from .	這是基地組織建立的地方 。
we also see a very strong insurgency embedded there .	我們也看到很強烈的暴動發生在那兒 。
so this terrorism concern is also part of the global commons , and what we must address .	所以 , 這種恐怖主義的擔憂 , 也是全球公有物的一部分 , 也是我們必須要處理的 。
so here we are , 21st century .	所以 , 在21世紀 ,
we know our 20thcentury tools are not going to work .	我們知道我們20世紀的工具是行不通的 。
what should we do ?	我們應該怎麼做 ?
i would argue that we will not deliver security solely from the barrel of a gun .	我主張 , 我們不能僅僅依靠一把槍來遞送安全 。
we will not deliver security solely from the barrel of a gun .	我們不能僅僅依靠槍支來遞送安全 。
we will need the application of military force .	我們會需要軍事力量的應用 。
when we do it , we must do it well , and competently .	當我們做到時 , 我們必須要做得很好 , 且要有能力 。
but my thesis is , opensource security is about international , interagency , privatepublic connection pulled together by this idea of strategic communication on the internet .	但我的論點是 , 開放式安全是關于國際的 , 跨部門的 , 私人和公共的聯系 , 通過互聯網溝通這個概念 , 將公開 。
let me give you a couple of examples of how this works in a positive way .	讓我舉幾個例子來說明這是如何運作的 , 以一個正面的方式 。
this is afghanistan . these are afghan soldiers .	這是阿富汗 。 這些是阿富汗士兵 。
they are all holding books .	他們都拿著書 。
you should say , " that's odd . i thought i read that this demographic , young men and women in their 20s and 30s , is largely illiterate in afghanistan . "	你應該說: 「 真奇怪 , 我以為我讀到過了這個人口統計學的年齡 , 20到30多歲 , 在阿富汗是不識字的 。 」
you would be correct .	你會是正確的 。
eightyfive percent cannot read when they enter the security forces of afghanistan .	當他們進入阿富汗的安全部隊時 , 85%不會閱讀 。
why ? because the taliban withheld education during the period of time in which these men and women would have learned to read .	為什麼 ? 因為在這段期間 , 塔利班接受了教育 , 這些男女都可以學會閱讀 。
so the question is , so , why are they all standing there holding books ?	所以問題是 , 為什麼他們都站在那裡拿書 ?
the answer is , we are teaching them to read in literacy courses by nato in partnership with private sector entities , in partnership with development agencies .	答案是 , 我們在北約和私營企業合作時 , 教導他們閱讀讀讀讀讀讀讀讀讀讀讀書 , 並且和發展署合作 。
we've taught well over 200 , 000 afghan security forces to read and write at a basic level .	我們已經教了超過二十萬的阿富汗安全部隊士兵以最基本的程度閱讀和寫字 。
when you can read and write in afghanistan , you will typically put a pen in your pocket .	當你能讀和寫在阿富汗時 , 通常就會放一支筆在口袋裡 。
at the ceremonies , when these young men and women graduate , they take that pen with great pride , and put it in their pocket .	在畢業典禮上 , 當這些年輕男女畢業時 , 她們帶著自豪的筆 , 把筆放進他們的口袋 。
this is bringing together international — there are 50 nations involved in this mission — interagency — these development agencies — and privatepublic , to take on this kind of security .	這就要把國際組織起來了 , 有五十個國家參與了這個任務 , 跨部門 , 這些發展機構 , 和私人和公共部門 , 共同進行這種安全的任務 。
now , we are also teaching them combat skills , of course , but i would argue , opensource security means connecting in ways that create longer lasting security effect .	當然 , 我們也在教他們格鬥技巧 , 但我要說 , 開放式安全意味著要用能夠創造更長久安全效應的方式來連結 。
this is a us navy warship .	這是美國海軍戰艦 。
it's called the comfort .	叫做舒適感 。
there's a sister ship called the mercy .	有一艘姊妹船叫做mercy號
they are hospital ships .	他們是醫院的船 。
this one , the comfort , operates throughout the caribbean and the coast of south america conducting patient treatments .	這一個 , 舒適 , 在加勒比海和南美洲的海岸進行病人的治療 。
on a typical cruise , they'll do 400 , 000 patient treatments .	在一般的情況下 , 他們會進行40萬次的治療 。
it is crewed not strictly by military but by a combination of humanitarian organizations: operation hope , project smile .	這部電影的船員不是嚴格的被軍事行動 , 而是結合人道組織:運營希望、計劃微笑 。
other organizations send volunteers .	其他組織送來志願者
interagency physicians come out .	各部落的醫師會出來 ,
they're all part of this .	他們都是這個的一部分 。
to give you one example of the impact this can have , this little boy , eight years old , walked with his mother two days to come to the eye clinic put on by the comfort .	舉個例子 , 這個小男孩 , 八歲 , 和他的媽媽走了兩天來到安慰號上的眼科診所 。
when he was fitted , over his extremely myopic eyes , he suddenly looked up and said , " mama , veo el mundo . "	當他被裝備好時 , 透過他極端的微妙眼睛 , 他突然抬頭 , 說: 「 媽媽 , veoelmundo 。 」
" mom , i see the world . "	「 媽媽 , 我看到世界了 。 」
multiply this by 400 , 000 patient treatments , this privatepublic collaboration with security forces , and you begin to see the power of creating security in a very different way .	把這個乘以400 , 000個病人治療 , 這個私人和公共的合作力量加上了安全力量 , 你就會開始看到創造安全的力量有多大不同 。
here you see baseball players .	這裡你看到棒球選手
can you pick out the two us army soldiers in this photograph ?	你能在這張照片裡挑出兩名美軍士兵嗎 ?
they are the two young men on either side of these young boys . this is part of a series of baseball clinics , where we have explored collaboration between major league baseball , the department of state , who sets up the diplomatic piece of this , military baseball players , who are real soldiers with real skills but participate in this mission , and they put on clinics throughout latin america and the caribbean , in honduras , in nicaragua , in all of the central american and caribbean nations where baseball is so popular , and it creates security .	他們是這群小男孩兩邊的小男孩 。 這是棒球診所的一部分 , 在那裡 , 我們一起探索了棒球大聯盟 , 國務院 , 設立了這些外交部門 , 軍隊棒球選手 , 他們是真正的士兵 , 用的是真正的技能 , 但他們參與了這項任務 , 把診所放在拉丁美洲和加勒比的加勒比 , 位在宏都拉斯 , 卡里加拉瓜 , 創造了所有中美洲 , 加勒比和加勒南部 。
it shows role models to young men and women about fitness and about life that i would argue help create security for us .	它向年輕男女展現榜樣 , 展現出體良和生命的重要性 , 我主張幫我們創造安全 。
another aspect of this partnership is in disaster relief .	這種合作的另一面在災難救援上 。
this is a us air force helicopter participating after the tsunami in 2004 which killed 250 , 000 people .	這是美國空軍的直升機 , 參與2004年海嘯後 , 造成25萬人死亡 。
in each of these major disasters — the tsunami in 2004 , 250 , 000 dead , the kashmiri earthquake in pakistan , 2005 , 85 , 000 dead , the haitian earthquake , about 300 , 000 dead , more recently the awful earthquaketsunami combination which struck japan and its nuclear industry — in all of these instances , we see partnerships between international actors , interagency , privatepublic working with security forces to respond to this kind of natural disaster .	在這些重大災難中2004年的海嘯 , 25萬人死亡 , 巴基斯坦的喀什米部落地震 , 2005年 , 8萬5千人死亡 , 海地震 , 30萬人的死亡 , 最近發生了可怕的地震災難 , 襲擊日本核工業 , 在所有這些例子中 , 我們看到了國際部門 , 跨部門 , 私人和公共部門 , 合作的安全 。
so these are examples of this idea of opensource security .	所以這些就是開放式安全理念的例子 。
we tie it together , increasingly , by doing things like this .	我們將它綁在一起 , 逐漸地 , 做成這樣的事情 。
now , you're looking at this thinking , " ah , admiral , these must be sea lanes of communication , or these might be fiber optic cables . "	現在 , 你看到的這個想法是 , " 啊 , 看啊 , 這些一定是通訊的海道 , 或者這些是光纖電纜 。 "
no . this is a graphic of the world according to twitter .	不 。 這張圖是根據推特所傳達的世界 。
purple are tweets . green are geolocation .	紫色是推特 。 綠色是地點分配 。
white is the synthesis .	白色是合成的 。
it's a perfect evocation of that great population survey , the six largest nations in the world in descending order: china , india , facebook , the united states , twitter and indonesia .	這是很棒的人口調查 , 六大國家依次排名世界 。 中國、印度、臉書、美國、推特 , 和印尼 。
why do we want to get in these nets ?	我們為什麼要買這些網子呢 ?
why do we want to be involved ?	我們為什麼想要參與其中呢 ?
we talked earlier about the arab spring , and the power of all this .	我們之前談到阿拉伯之春 , 以及這一切的力量 。
i'll give you another example , and it's how you move this message .	我再舉一個例子 , 就是你如何移動這個訊息 。
i gave a talk like this in london a while back about this point . i said , as i say to all of you , i'm on facebook . friend me .	我在倫敦發表了這樣一個演講 , 講到這個 。 我對你們說 , 我在facebook上 , 親愛的 。
got a little laugh from the audience .	聽眾的笑聲 。
there was an article which was run by ap , on the wire .	當時有一篇ap的文章 , 在線上負責管理 。
got picked up in two places in the world: finland and indonesia .	被帶到世界上兩個地方:芬蘭和印尼 。
the headline was: nato admiral needs friends .	標題是:北約大都會需要朋友 。
and the story was a catalyst , and the next morning i had hundreds of facebook friend requests from indonesians and finns , mostly saying , " admiral , we heard you need a friend , and oh , by the way , what is nato ? "	故事是一名催化劑第二天早上我就有了上百個facebook好友請求 , 來自印尼和芬蘭多半的請求 , 主要是說: 「 司令 , 我們聽說你需要一位朋友 , 喔 , 對了 , nato是哪位 ? 」
yeah , we laugh , but this is how we move the message , and moving that message is how we connect international , interagency , privatepublic , and these social nets to help create security .	是啊 , 我們笑了 , 但這就是我們如何移動訊息 , 移動那個訊息就是我們如何連結國際 , 跨部門 , 私人和公共 , 還有這些社群網絡 , 來協助創造安全 。
now , let me hit a somber note .	現在 , 我來談談一個嚴肅的事實 。
this is a photograph of a brave british soldier .	這張照片是一位勇敢的英國士兵 。
he's in the scots guards .	他在蘇格蘭衛隊
he's standing the watch in helmand , in southern afghanistan .	他正在helmand站崗 , 在阿富汗南部 。
i put him here to remind us , i would not want anyone to leave the room thinking that we do not need capable , competent militaries who can create real military effect .	我把他放到這裡來提醒我們 , 我不希望有人離開房間 , 認為我們不需要能夠創造真正的軍事力量 。
that is the core of who we are and what we do , and we do it to protect freedom , freedom of speech , all the things we treasure in our societies .	這才是我們的核心 , 也是我們所做的 , 我們為了保護自由 , 言論自由 , 和所有我們在社會中珍視的 。
but , you know , life is not an onandoff switch .	但是 , 你知道 , 生活不是一個開關 。
you don't have to have a military that is either in hard combat or is in the barracks .	你不需要有一支軍隊 , 不是在戰鬥中 , 就是在營區裡 。
i would argue life is a rheostat .	我會主張生命是一種 「 修辭 」 。
you have to dial it in , and as i think about how we create security in this 21st century , there will be times when we will apply hard power in true war and crisis , but there will be many instances , as we've talked about today , where our militaries can be part of creating 21stcentury security , international , interagency , privatepublic , connected with competent communication .	你要調一個數值 , 並且正如我思考我們如何在21世紀制造安全一樣 , 有時候我們在真正的戰爭和危機中運用硬實力 , 但是會有很多的例子 , 正如我們今天所談到的 , 我們的軍隊可以成為創造21世紀安全的一部分 , 國際的 , 跨部門的 , 公私的 , 與極端的溝通聯繫起來 。
i would close by saying that we heard earlier today about wikipedia . i use wikipedia all the time to look up facts , and as all of you appreciate , wikipedia is not created by 12 brilliant people locked in a room writing articles .	最後我要說的是 , 今天早些時候我就聽到維基百科 。 我經常使用維基百科查事實 , 正如你們所有人都很欣賞維基百科 , 並不是靠12個聰明的人把自己關在屋子裡寫文章創造出來的 。
wikipedia , every day , is tens of thousands of people inputting information , and every day millions of people withdrawing that information .	維基百科每天都有成千上萬的人輸入資料每天有數百萬人會收到這些資訊
it's a perfect image for the fundamental point that no one of us is as smart as all of us thinking together .	它是一個完美的圖像 , 可以代表我們當中沒有人像所有人一樣聰明 , 一樣一起思考 。
no one person , no one alliance , no one nation , no one of us is as smart as all of us thinking together .	沒有一個人 , 沒有一個聯盟 , 沒有一個國家是如此地聰明 , 像我們所有人一起思考一樣 。
the vision statement of wikipedia is very simple: a world in which every human being can freely share in the sum of all knowledge .	維基百科的願景說得很簡單:一個每個人都可以自由地分享所有知識的世界 。
my thesis for you is that by combining international , interagency , privatepublic , strategic communication , together , in this 21st century , we can create the sum of all security .	我的論點是 , 藉由結合國際 , 跨部門 , 公私的和平 , 戰略通信 , 共同在21世紀 , 我們就能創造出全部安全的總和 。
thank you very much . thank you . thank you .	非常感謝 。 謝謝 。 謝謝 。 謝謝 。
